<script type="text/javascript">
(function (retailrocket) {
  'use strict';

  if (!('duplicates' in retailrocket.modules)) {
    retailrocket.setModule('duplicates', [], function () {
      var savedIds = [];
      var paramName = 'ItemId';

      function has(id) {
        return (savedIds.indexOf(id) !== -1);
      }

      function add(id) {
        savedIds = savedIds.concat(id);
      }

      function remove(id) {
        var ids = [].concat(id);

        savedIds = savedIds.filter(function (savedId) {
          return ids.indexOf(savedId) === -1;
        });
      }

      function filter(recom) {
        if (!recom[paramName]) {
          return true;
        }

        if (!has(recom[paramName])) {
          add(recom[paramName]);
          return true;
        }

        return false;
      }

      function filteredCount(recoms) {
        return recoms.reduce(function (acc, recom) {
          return (acc + (has(recom[paramName]) ? 1 : 0));
        }, 0);
      }

      function getItems() {
        return savedIds.slice();
      }

      return {
        has: has,
        add: add,
        remove: remove,
        filter: filter,
        filteredCount: filteredCount,
        getItems: getItems,
      };
    });
  }

  retailrocket['rbt570f96655a6589145c15de74'] = (function () {
    
    function checkData (rrItems) {
      var date = Date.now();
      var checkTime = false;
      var hiddenTimeAttr = rrItems.getAttribute('data-hidden-time').split(';');

      hiddenTimeAttr.forEach(function (item) {
        var time = item.split('/');
        var timeBefore = Date.parse(time[0]);
        var timeAfter = Date.parse(time[1]);

        if (date >= timeBefore && date <= timeAfter) {
          checkTime = true;
        }
      });

      if (checkTime) {
        rrItems.classList.add('rr-hidden-price');
      }
    }
    
    function preRenderFn(widget, recoms, renderFn) {
      var filteredRecoms = recoms.filter(retailrocket.modules.duplicates.filter);

      if (filteredRecoms.length > 0) {
        renderFn(filteredRecoms);
      } else {
        retailrocket.widget.render(widget.getAttribute('data-next-render'));
      }
    }
    
    function postRenderFn(widget) {
      checkData(widget.querySelector('.retailrocket-items'));
    }

    return {
      preRenderFn: preRenderFn,
      postRenderFn: postRenderFn
    };
  }());

  retailrocket.widget.render('rr-widget-570f96655a6589145c15de74-search');
}(retailrocket));
